" ’’tippaniyan Rai said that the public auditor is also engaged in improving the work of governmental administration and administration in the same way as other agencies of administration are engaged in this work
 unhone kaha ‘‘lekhapariksha karte hue ham apane ko unki tarah nahin balki khud ko unke sthaan par bithakar sthitiyon ko dekhte hai

 ’’ Rai said that public auditors who audit the use of public money should be objective and credible
 unhone kaha ‘‘ham tabhi vishwaas hasil kar sakate hai jab hamaari behatar saakh hogi, sakasham honge or niyantranmukt honge

 ’’ Rai advised the government that if it wants to help, it should help the enterprises and not the individuals called entrepreneurs

 ’’ CAG Vinod Rai, who exposed the flaws in the 2G allocation in the telecom sector and the flaws in the allocation of coal mines through his report, has also faced criticism from the government over the reports but says the role of public auditor is only in Parliament
 It should not be limited to presenting the report
 vinod raay ne savaalie lahaze main kaha ‘‘lok lekhapareekshak hone ke naate kya hamen keval sansad main apni report pesh karne tak hi apni bhoomika simit rakhni chahie yaa phir isse aage badhanaa chahie visheshkar aise maamalon main, jahaan gramin swasthya, praathmik shiksha, jal pradooshan, paryaavaran or peyajal se jude mudde he, unpar kshetron main apni lekha pariksha tippaniyon ke sambandh main aam janata ko bhi jaagrit karnaa chahie
 On the issue of the CAG crossing its jurisdiction, Rai believes that Indian democracy is maturing now and the urban middle class is now taking more interest in matters related to the civic sector
 The public is the biggest contributor to the expenditure, we will continue on the new path
 ’’ Rai said that audit of government and public establishments increases trust in society and has a positive effect
 raay ke anusaar ‘‘lekha pariksha yani audit se sarkaar ke saarvajanik kosh se dhan kaa istemaal karne waalon ko ehtiyaat rahati he ki lekhapariksha hone ke baad janata ko unke kaamkaaj ke taur tareeke ke bare main pataa chal jaayegaa

 Chewing nails is a bad habit
 bachche to bachche kai bade bhi iske lati hote hai
 In health terms, it is a dirty habit that can make a person sick
 persenality exparts kaa maananaa hai ki ye persenality sambandhi beemaari he
 However, it starts in childhood
 aise main agar maa-baap chahen to bachche kii is aadat ko sudhaar bhi sakate hai
 Here are some home remedies that you can get rid of from this child's bad addiction
 1
 The bitter taste of neem oil neem will prevent your child from chewing nails
 saath hi ye acha antiseptic he to aapke baccha sankramak bimariyon se bhi bachaa rahegaa
 With the help of cotton swabs, apply neem oil on the fingers of the child
 ye kuch der baad khud hi suukh jayega
 Due to addiction, as soon as the child's finger goes in the mouth, he will feel bitter and he will remove the finger
 2
 Garlic garlic is another remedy
 ye bhi aapke bachche ko nakhun chabane kii buree lat se raahat dilaa saktaa he
 Cut some garlic cloves and rub on the fingers and nails of the child
 agar aap chahen to lahasun kaa tel bhi laga sakati hai
 The taste and smell of garlic will prove helpful in reducing this habit of your child
 3
 Bitter gourd is also very beneficial for children who chew nails
 aap ghar par iskaa paste bana len or iske ras ko bachche ke nakhun par laga den
 The bitter taste of bitter gourd will help the child to get rid of this bad addiction
 4
 Keep the nails short
 It depends entirely on your vigilance that as soon as the baby's nails grow, you cut them
 aisa karne se uski ye aadat chhot jaaegi
 5
 nakli nakhunbazar main plastic ke nakhun milte hai
 Those are affixed to natural nails
 jab baccha ungliyaan munh main daalata he to uske munh main plastic ke nakhun aate hai
 Even with this effort, you can overcome this child's bad addiction
 6
 Wear gloves: You can also keep the child wearing gloves if you want
 aisa karne se ungliyaan sidhe uske munh main nahin jaaengi or wo nakhun nahin chaba paaegaa
 7
 duusari gatividhiyon main uljhakarbache ko zyada se zyada vyast rakhane kii koshish karen
 This will distract his attention and he will forget to chew the nails
